</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Touch Targets</h4><a id="user-content-touch-targets" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Touch Targets" href="#touch-targets"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>button-primary</code> pill renders at ~32 px tall in nav and ~48 px tall in marketing contexts. Marketing CTAs comfortably meet WCAG AAA at all breakpoints; nav buttons inflate touch area through <code>{spacing.xs}</code> padding on mobile to meet the 44 × 44 px floor.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Collapsing Strategy</h4><a id="user-content-collapsing-strategy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Collapsing Strategy" href="#collapsing-strategy"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Nav</strong>: full link row + Ask AI / Log In / Sign Up pills at desktop. Collapses to logo + hamburger at mobile with the menu opening as a full-overlay.</li>
<li><strong>Hero</strong>: mesh gradient stays centred; headline + body stack vertically at all breakpoints (the brand doesn't use a split-hero pattern).</li>
<li><strong>Three-feature row</strong>: 3-up → 2-up → 1-up at the breakpoints above; cards keep their <code>{rounded.md}</code> 8 px shape across all viewports.</li>
<li><strong>Pricing card grid</strong>: 3-up at desktop, vertical stack at mobile with <code>pricing-card-featured</code> always sitting in the middle.</li>
<li><strong>Template grid</strong>: 5-up → 3-up → 2-up → 1-up. Each <code>template-card</code> keeps its 16:9 aspect on the image.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Image Behavior</h4><a id="user-content-image-behavior" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Image Behavior" href="#image-behavior"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Mesh gradient</strong>: rendered as inline SVG or canvas-painted gradient; scales fluidly with the hero container; never crops, never tiles.</li>
<li><strong>Customer logos</strong>: rendered as monochrome SVGs in the logo strip; consistent 24 px height.</li>
<li><strong>Code editor mockup</strong>: dark <code>{colors.primary}</code> rectangle with mono text rendered inside; treated as an image at the layout level.</li>
<li><strong>Template thumbnails</strong>: 16:9 landscape inside <code>{rounded.md}</code> card chrome; lazy-loaded; consistent grayscale palette in the placeholder state.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Elevation &amp; Depth</h2><a id="user-content-elevation--depth" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Elevation &amp; Depth" href="#elevation--depth"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Level</th>
<th>Treatment</th>
<th>Use</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Level 0 — Flat</td>
<td>No shadow, no border.</td>
<td>Full-bleed hero bands and the polarity-flipped dark sections.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Level 1 — Inset Hairline</td>
<td><code>0 0 0 1px #00000014</code> inset 1 px border.</td>
<td>Default card chrome — the brand's universal "you can see this card" cue.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Level 2 — Subtle Drop</td>
<td><code>0px 1px 1px #00000005, 0px 2px 2px #0000000a</code> plus inset hairline.</td>
<td>Slightly elevated cards (template-grid, marketing-card).</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Level 3 — Soft Stack</td>
<td><code>0px 2px 2px #0000000a, 0px 8px 8px -8px #0000000a</code> plus inset hairline.</td>
<td>The "medium" elevation — feature-grid cards.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Level 4 — Float Stack</td>
<td><code>0px 2px 2px #0000000a, 0px 8px 16px -4px #0000000a</code> plus inset hairline.</td>
<td>"Large" elevation — pricing cards, callout panels.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Level 5 — Modal</td>
<td><code>0px 1px 1px #00000005, 0px 8px 16px -4px #0000000a, 0px 24px 32px -8px #0000000f</code> plus inset hairline.</td>
<td>Modal / dialog surfaces and dropdown menus.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto">The brand uses STACKED shadows — multiple small offsets layered to fake natural light — never a single 8-px-blur generic drop. Inset hairline rings are always added so the card edge stays crisp.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Decorative Depth</h3><a id="user-content-decorative-depth" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Decorative Depth" href="#decorative-depth"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Mesh gradient as atmospheric depth</strong>: the hero's multi-stop gradient is the brand's only "atmospheric" effect — applied as a flat 2-D backdrop rather than a 3-D illustration.</li>
<li><strong>Polarity-flipped dark band as section-depth</strong>: switching the surface from <code>{colors.canvas-soft}</code> to <code>{colors.primary}</code> (the deep ink) is the brand's chief depth cue between bands.</li>
<li><strong>Inset-shadow + drop-shadow combo</strong>: the cards' combination of an inset 1 px ring and a multi-stop drop produces a "card sits on the page" effect without ever feeling material-heavy.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Shapes</h2><a id="user-content-shapes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Shapes" href="#shapes"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Border Radius Scale</h3><a id="user-content-border-radius-scale" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Border Radius Scale" href="#border-radius-scale"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Photography Geometry</h3><a id="user-content-photography-geometry" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Photography Geometry" href="#photography-geometry"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Mesh gradient</strong>: full-bleed 2-D atmospheric backdrop, never cropped to a frame; treated as the page's wallpaper.</li>
<li><strong>Customer logos</strong>: monochrome SVG, consistent 24 px height in a flex row.</li>
<li><strong>Code editor mockup</strong>: 16:10 dark rectangle, <code>{rounded.md}</code> corners.</li>
<li><strong>Template thumbnails</strong>: 16:9 landscape inside <code>{rounded.md}</code> chrome.</li>
<li><strong>Showcase imagery</strong>: 2:1 or 16:9 inside <code>{rounded.lg}</code> to <code>{rounded.xl}</code> chrome with a stacked shadow.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Components</h2><a id="user-content-components" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Components" href="#components"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Buttons</h3><a id="user-content-buttons" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Buttons" href="#buttons"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>button-primary</code></strong> — the canonical 100-px-radius black pill, marketing scale.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.primary}</code>, text <code>{colors.on-primary}</code>, label set in <code>{typography.button-lg}</code>, padding <code>0px {spacing.sm}</code> 12 px, shape <code>{rounded.pill}</code> 100 px. Renders ~48 px tall when paired with the marketing flex layout.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>button-secondary</code></strong> — the white pill paired with the black primary inside marketing bands.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, same typography + padding as <code>button-primary</code>, shape <code>{rounded.pill}</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>button-primary-sm</code></strong> — the smaller-scale primary pill used inside nav and pricing-card CTAs.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.primary}</code>, text <code>{colors.on-primary}</code>, label set in <code>{typography.button-md}</code> (14 px / 500), shape <code>{rounded.pill}</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>button-secondary-sm</code></strong> — the smaller-scale white pill paired with <code>button-primary-sm</code>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, same typography + shape as <code>button-primary-sm</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>tab-ghost</code></strong> — the centred-row tab pill ("AI Apps / Web Apps / Ecommerce / Marketing / Platforms").</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, label set in <code>{typography.body-sm}</code>, padding <code>0px {spacing.md}</code>, shape <code>{rounded.pill-sm}</code> 64 px.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>icon-button-circular</code></strong> — the circular icon container (often a "?" or arrow inside).</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, dark icon, 1 px solid hairline border, shape <code>{rounded.full}</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Nav CTAs:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>nav-cta-signup</code></strong> — the small black "Sign Up" button in the nav row.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.primary}</code>, text <code>{colors.on-primary}</code>, label <code>{typography.body-sm-strong}</code>, padding <code>0px {spacing.xs}</code>, height 28 px, shape <code>{rounded.sm}</code> 6 px (the brand's <code>--geist-radius</code>).</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>nav-cta-login</code></strong> — the white "Log In" button in the nav.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, same typography / height / shape as <code>nav-cta-signup</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>nav-cta-ask-ai</code></strong> — the small "Ask AI" button with a faint border.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, 1 px solid <code>{colors.hairline}</code> border (extracted as <code>0px solid rgb(235, 235, 235)</code>), same typography / height / shape.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Cards &amp; Containers</h3><a id="user-content-cards--containers" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Cards &amp; Containers" href="#cards--containers"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>card-marketing</code></strong> — the canonical marketing feature card (3-up section cards).</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, padding <code>{spacing.lg}</code> 24 px, shape <code>{rounded.md}</code> 8 px (the <code>--geist-marketing-radius</code>). Carries Level 3 soft-stack shadow.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>card-marketing-large</code></strong> — the larger marketing card used for "compute model" / "AI Gateway" callouts.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, padding <code>{spacing.xl}</code>, shape <code>{rounded.lg}</code> 12 px. Carries Level 4 float-stack shadow.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>card-soft</code></strong> — the soft-tinted card used inside cluster groups (lighter than canvas-soft).</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas-soft}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, padding <code>{spacing.lg}</code>, shape <code>{rounded.md}</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>template-card</code></strong> — the deploy-template card in the "Deploy your first app" grid.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, padding <code>{spacing.md}</code> 16 px, shape <code>{rounded.md}</code> 8 px. Hosts a 16:9 thumbnail at the top.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>code-editor-mockup</code></strong> — the dark code-preview surface inside marketing bands.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.primary}</code>, text <code>{colors.on-primary}</code>, body in <code>{typography.code}</code> (13 px / Geist Mono), padding <code>{spacing.lg}</code> 24 px, shape <code>{rounded.md}</code> 8 px.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>pricing-card</code></strong> — the default pricing-tier card.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, padding <code>{spacing.xl}</code> 32 px, shape <code>{rounded.lg}</code> 12 px. Inside: tier name in <code>{typography.display-md}</code>, price in <code>{typography.display-xl}</code>, feature list in <code>{typography.body-md}</code> rows, CTA at the bottom.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>pricing-card-featured</code></strong> — the polarity-flipped "Pro" tier card.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.primary}</code>, text <code>{colors.on-primary}</code>, same shape + padding as <code>pricing-card</code>. CTA inverts to <code>button-secondary-sm</code> (white pill on black card).</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Inputs &amp; Forms</h3><a id="user-content-inputs--forms" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Inputs &amp; Forms" href="#inputs--forms"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>form-input</code></strong> — the canonical text input.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, 1 px solid <code>{colors.hairline}</code> border, body in <code>{typography.body-sm}</code> (14 px), padding <code>0px {spacing.sm}</code>, height 40 px (the brand's <code>--geist-form-height</code>), shape <code>{rounded.sm}</code> 6 px.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>form-input-sm</code></strong> — small-height variant (32 px tall) for tight forms.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Same as <code>form-input</code> but height 32 px (the <code>--geist-form-small-height</code>).</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>form-input-lg</code></strong> — large-height variant (48 px tall) for hero CTAs.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Same as <code>form-input</code> but height 48 px (the <code>--geist-form-large-height</code>); body in <code>{typography.body-md}</code> 16 px.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Navigation</h3><a id="user-content-navigation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Navigation" href="#navigation"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>nav-bar</code></strong> — the sticky top nav.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, height 64 px (the brand's <code>--header-height</code>), padding <code>{spacing.sm} {spacing.lg}</code>. Layout: logo left, link row centre, "Ask AI / Log In / Sign Up" cluster right.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>nav-link</code></strong> — the centred link row inside <code>nav-bar</code>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Text <code>{colors.body}</code>, set in <code>{typography.body-sm}</code>, padding <code>{spacing.xs} {spacing.sm}</code>, shape <code>{rounded.full}</code> (ghost pill — visible only on hover or active, but the radius is documented).</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>footer</code></strong> — the bottom 4-column nav.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.body}</code>, padding <code>{spacing.4xl} {spacing.lg}</code>. Eyebrow column labels in <code>{typography.caption-mono}</code> (uppercase mono effect); link rows in <code>{typography.body-sm}</code>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Signature Components</h3><a id="user-content-signature-components" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Signature Components" href="#signature-components"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>hero-band</code></strong> — the white hero with the mesh gradient backdrop.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code> (or <code>{colors.canvas-soft}</code> on some surfaces), text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, padding <code>{spacing.4xl} {spacing.lg}</code>. Inside: a small mono badge above the headline, the headline in <code>{typography.display-xl}</code> (sentence-case, period-terminated), a body lead in <code>{typography.body-lg}</code>, then a CTA row with <code>button-primary</code> + <code>button-secondary</code>. The mesh gradient sits behind, scaled to occupy roughly the top half of the band.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>feature-mesh-band</code></strong> — the secondary section that hosts a mesh-gradient atmospheric backdrop with feature copy on top.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, padding <code>{spacing.5xl} {spacing.lg}</code>. Section headline in <code>{typography.display-lg}</code>; supporting body in <code>{typography.body-md}</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>showcase-band-light</code></strong> — a soft-canvas section ("Deploy your first app in seconds").</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas-soft}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, padding <code>{spacing.5xl} {spacing.lg}</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>showcase-band-dark</code></strong> — the polarity-flipped dark band ("A compute model for all workloads").</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.primary}</code>, text <code>{colors.on-primary}</code>, padding <code>{spacing.5xl} {spacing.lg}</code>. Section headline in <code>{typography.display-lg}</code> (white on black). Often contains a <code>code-editor-mockup</code> flush with the band.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>logo-strip</code></strong> — the customer-logo wrapping row near the top of the page.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.body}</code>, padding <code>{spacing.lg} {spacing.xl}</code>. Logos rendered as monochrome SVGs at consistent height.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>badge-secondary</code></strong> — the small inline metadata pill ("New", "Beta", "Live").</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas-soft}</code>, text <code>{colors.body}</code>, body in <code>{typography.caption}</code>, padding <code>0px {spacing.xs}</code>, shape <code>{rounded.full}</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>banner-marketing</code></strong> — the "Introducing X" announcement pill at the top of pages.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Background <code>{colors.canvas-soft}</code>, text <code>{colors.body}</code>, body in <code>{typography.body-sm}</code>, padding <code>{spacing.xs} {spacing.sm}</code>, shape <code>{rounded.full}</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>link-inline</code></strong> — body-copy inline links.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Text <code>{colors.link}</code> (<code>#0070f3</code>), body in <code>{typography.body-md}</code>, underlined.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Examples (illustrative)</h3><a id="user-content-examples-illustrative" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Examples (illustrative)" href="#examples-illustrative"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Auto-derived kit-mirror demonstration surfaces (<code>scripts/derive-examples-block.mjs</code>). Each <code>ex-*</code> entry references brand-native primitives so downstream consumers (<code>/preview-design</code>, <code>/generate-kit</code>) re-skin the same 10 surfaces consistently. <code>TO_FILL</code> markers indicate missing primitives — resolve in the LLM judgment pass.</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>ex-pricing-tier</code></strong> — Default Pricing tier card. Re-uses feature-card chrome with brand canvas-soft surface.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Properties: <code>backgroundColor</code>, <code>textColor</code>, <code>borderColor</code>, <code>rounded</code>, <code>padding</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>ex-pricing-tier-featured</code></strong> — Featured/highlighted tier — polarity-flipped surface (dark fill + light text in light mode, light fill + dark text in dark mode).</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Properties: <code>backgroundColor</code>, <code>textColor</code>, <code>rounded</code>, <code>padding</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>ex-product-selector</code></strong> — What's Included summary card — re-purposed for SaaS / B2B verticals (NOT a literal product gallery).</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Properties: <code>backgroundColor</code>, <code>rounded</code>, <code>padding</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>ex-cart-drawer</code></strong> — Subscription summary — re-purposed for SaaS / B2B (line items per add-on, not literal cart).</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Properties: <code>backgroundColor</code>, <code>rounded</code>, <code>padding</code>, <code>item-divider</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>ex-app-shell-row</code></strong> — Sidebar nav row inside the App Shell example. Active state uses brand primary as the indicator.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Properties: <code>backgroundColor</code>, <code>activeIndicator</code>, <code>rounded</code>, <code>padding</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>ex-data-table-cell</code></strong> — Default data-table th + td chrome. Header uses mono-caps eyebrow typography; body uses body-sm.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Properties: <code>headerBackground</code>, <code>headerTypography</code>, <code>bodyTypography</code>, <code>cellPadding</code>, <code>rowBorder</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>ex-auth-form-card</code></strong> — Sign-in / sign-up card. Re-uses feature-card chrome with text-input primitives inside.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Properties: <code>backgroundColor</code>, <code>rounded</code>, <code>padding</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>ex-modal-card</code></strong> — Modal dialog surface — same chrome as feature-card with elevated shadow.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Properties: <code>backgroundColor</code>, <code>rounded</code>, <code>padding</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>ex-empty-state-card</code></strong> — Empty-state illustration frame.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Properties: <code>backgroundColor</code>, <code>rounded</code>, <code>padding</code>, <code>captionTypography</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>ex-toast</code></strong> — Toast notification surface — feature-card shape + medium shadow.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Properties: <code>backgroundColor</code>, <code>rounded</code>, <code>padding</code>, <code>typography</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Do's and Don'ts</h2><a id="user-content-dos-and-donts" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Do's and Don'ts" href="#dos-and-donts"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Do</h3><a id="user-content-do" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Do" href="#do"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Reserve <code>{colors.primary}</code> (<code>#171717</code>) for primary CTAs across the page. Black ink IS the conversion target.</li>
<li>Use <code>{rounded.pill}</code> 100 px for every marketing-scale CTA and <code>{rounded.sm}</code> 6 px for nav-scale buttons. The two pill scales coexist deliberately.</li>
<li>Set every headline in <code>{typography.display-*}</code> weight 600, sentence-case, often period-terminated. Aggressive negative tracking is part of the voice.</li>
<li>Use the brand mesh gradient as atmospheric decoration at hero scale only — never miniaturise it to an icon, never reduce to a single colour.</li>
<li>Layer stacked shadows (multiple small offsets with inset hairline) rather than single heavy drops. The brand's elevation is calmer than Material.</li>
<li>Cycle page surfaces in <code>{colors.canvas-soft}</code> → <code>{colors.canvas}</code> → <code>{colors.primary}</code> polarity-flipped bands; the dark band IS the depth cue.</li>
<li>Set every code block and technical eyebrow in <code>{typography.code}</code> / <code>{typography.caption-mono}</code>. Mono is the voice of the platform.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Don't</h3><a id="user-content-dont" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Don't" href="#dont"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Don't introduce a sixth accent colour. The brand operates with ink + gray + the four-pair gradient palette; new accents flatten the voice.</li>
<li>Don't render headlines in all-caps. Sentence-case + negative tracking is non-negotiable.</li>
<li>Don't drop a single heavy drop-shadow on cards. The brand's elevation is built from stacked small offsets + inset hairline rings.</li>
<li>Don't render the brand gradient at icon scale or in a single-colour reduced form. The gradient lives at hero scale only.</li>
<li>Don't promote the geometric sans to weight 700. The brand's display ceiling is 600.</li>
<li>Don't pair the marketing 100-px pill CTA shape with the 6-px nav radius on the same screen — pick a scale and stay there.</li>
<li>Don't set body paragraphs in the mono face. The mono is for code + technical labels only.</li>
</ul>
</article></div><div class="d-none"></div></section></div></div></div> </div> <!-- --> </div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="ScrollMarksContainer-module__scrollMarksContainer__Eu7uU" id="find-result-marks-container"></div><div class="d-none"></div><div class="d-none"></div></div> <!-- --> <!-- --> </div>
</react-app>




  </div>

</turbo-frame>

    </main>
  </div>

  </div>

    <template id="site-details-dialog">
